/************************************************************************
**
**		TRON 2000: 'You mama is so old she once built an altair' FX Attributes file
**
** This file contains the following special fx related definitions:
**
**	BeamFX,
**	DLightFX,
**	FireFX,
**	ImpactFX,
**	MuzzleFX,
**	ParticleMuzzleFX,
**	PExplFX,
**	PolyDebrisFX,
**	ProjectileFX,
**	PShowerFX,
**	PusherFX,
**	PVFX,
**	ScaleFX,
**	SoundFX,
**	TracerFX,
**	SprinkleFX
**
**
** NOTES:
**
**	1) All definition properties (i.e., DLightFX0) ARE case sensitive.
**	   If you are adding a new definition, it is best to start with a
**	   copy of an existing (working) definition.
**	2) Name properties are NOT case sensitive (i.e., Name = "Joe" is the same
**	   as Name = "JOE")
**	3) All time is specified in seconds (unless otherwise noted)
**	4) The Float type is the same as Real (i.e., 1.0 or 1.5)
**	5) The valid range of all RGB color properties is between
**	   0 and 255 (e.g., (0, 255, 0) would be green).
*/



/************************************************************************
**
** IMPACTFX
**
** ImpactFX definitions specify the properties making up an impact fx.
**
** All ImpactFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name used in Weapons.txt file.
**
**	CreateMark (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if a mark (bullethole or other mark) should be created
**		for this fx (1 = true, 0 = false).
**
**	ImpactOnSky (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if the fx should be done even if a surface wasn't
**		impacted (1 = true, 0 = false).
**
**	IgnoreFlesh (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if the fx should be ignored if the impact surface is
**		flesh (1 = true, 0 = false).  NOTE: The Impact sound and Pushers
**		are still created.
**
**	IgnoreLiquid (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if the fx should be ignored if the impact surface is
**		liquid (1 = true, 0 = false).  NOTE: The Impact sound and Pushers
**		are still created.
**
**	DoSurfaceFX (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if surface related fx (see Surface.txt) should be done
**		for this ImpactFX type (1 = true, 0 = false).
**
**	ScreenTint (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if the screen should be tinted (1 = true, 0 = false).
**
**	BlastMark (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if a blast mark should be created (1 = true, 0 = false).
**
**	Sound (String)
**
**		Specifies the impact sound.  Use the string "surface" to indicate
**		impacts based on surface and weapon type.
**
**	SoundRadius (Integer)
**
**		Specifies the radius at which the impact sound is played
**
**	AISoundRadius (Integer)
**
**		Specifies the radius at which the impact sound is heard by AI's
**
**	AIIgnoreSurface (Boolean)
**
**		True/false of whether the AISoundRadius should ignore the surface modifier
**		(useful for explosion-type impacts)
**
**  AIStimulusType (String)
**
**       Name of audio stimulus type created this impact. Should be set to
**       "EnemyWeaponImpactSound" or "EnemyDisturbanceSound".
**
**  AIAlarmLevel (Integer)
**
**       How alarming hearing the weapon impact is to an AI. Correponds
**       to thresholds set in AIBrains in aibutes.txt.
**
**	Mark (String)
**
**		Specifies the mark sprite.	Use the string "surface" to indicate
**		impacts based on surface and weapon type.
**
**	MarkScale (Float)
**
**		Specifies the scale of the mark sprite.
**
**	TintColor (Vector)
**
**		Specifies the color of the screen tint.
**
**	TintRampUp (Float)
**
**		Specifies the time for the screen tint to ramp up to the max intensity.
**
**	TintRampDown (Float)
**
**		Specifies the time for the screen tint to ramp down from the max intensity.
**
**	TintMaxTime (Float)
**
**		Specifies the time for the screen tint to stay at the max intensity.
**
**	BlastColor (Vector)
**
**		Specifies the color of the blast mark light.
**
**	BlastTimeMin (Float)
**
**		Specifies the min time for the blast mark to stay at its max intensity
**		(the actual time will be a random value between BlastTimeMin and
**		BlastTimeMax)
**
**	BlastTimeMax (Float)
**
**		Specifies the max time for the blast mark to stay at its max intensity.
**		(the actual time will be a random value between BlastTimeMin and
**		BlastTimeMax)
**
**	BlastFadeMin (Float)
**
**		Specifies the min time it will take the blast mark to fade away.
**		(the actual time will be a random value between BlastFadeMin and
**		BlastFadeMax)
**
**	BlastFadeMax (Float)
**
**		Specifies the max time it will take the blast mark to fade away.
**		(the actual time will be a random value between BlastFadeMin and
**		BlastFadeMax)
**
**	PusherName (String)  (OPTIONAL)
**
**		Specifies the optional name of a pusher fx to create for this impact.
**		The value of this property MUST correspond to the name of a PusherFX
**		record defined in the bellow.
**
**	FXName (String) (OPTIONAL)
**
**		Specifies the optional name of a FxED created FX to create for this impact.
**		The value of this property MUST correspond to the name of a FX created using FxED.
**		For example:
**
**			FxName = "StoneImpactFX01"
**
**
*/


/*
** ImpactFX - DiscImpact
*/

[ImpactFX0]

Name			= "DiscImpact"
CreateMark		= 1
ImpactOnSky 	= 0
IgnoreFlesh 	= 0
IgnoreLiquid	= 1
DoSurfaceFX 	= 1
ScreenTint		= 0
BlastMark		= 0
Sound			= ""
SoundRadius 	= 500
AISoundRadius	= 500
AIIgnoreSurface = 0
AIStimulusType  = "EnemyWeaponImpactSound"
AIAlarmLevel    = 5
Mark			= "surface" // Use surface texture flags
MarkScale		= 0.075000
TintColor		= <0.000000, 0.000000, 0.000000>
TintRampUp		= 0
TintRampDown	= 0
TintMaxTime 	= 0
BlastColor		= <0.000000, 0.000000, 0.000000>
BlastTimeMin	= 0
BlastTimeMax	= 0
BlastFadeMin	= 0
BlastFadeMax	= 0
PusherName		= ""
FXName			= "DISC_impact"

/************************************************************************
**
** FIREFX
**
** FireFX definitions specify the properties making up a fire fx
** record.	This record is used to determine the attributes for a
** given fire (i.e., weapon discharge) fx.
**
** All FireFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name used in Weapons.txt file.
**
**	FXName (String)
**
**		Name of an FxED created FX that will play at the fire pos.
**
**	EjectShells (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if shells should be created. (1 = true, 0 = false).
**
**	FireSound (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if a fire sound should be created.
**		(1 = true, 0 = false).
**
**	ExitMark (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if an exit mark (when exiting surface) should be
**		created. (1 = true, 0 = false).
**
**	ExitDebris (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if an exit debris (when exiting surface) should be
**		created. (1 = true, 0 = false).
**
**	ShellModel (String)
**
**		Name of the shell model associated with the fx (Flag 1024 only).
**
**	ShellSkin (String)
**
**		Name of the shell model skin associated with the fx (Flag 1024 only).
**
**	ShellScale (Vector)
**
**		Value to scale the shell model by (Flag 1024 only)
**
**	OldStyleBeamName# (String)	(OPTIONAL)
**
**		Specifies the optional name of a beam fx to create for this fire fx.
**		The value of this property MUST correspond to the name of a BeamFX
**		record defined in this file.  If the fire fx uses multiple beam fx
**		types, you may specify multiple BeamFXName properties.	For example:
**
**			OldStyleBeamName0	= "Red Laser"
**			OldStyleBeamName1	= "Blue Laser"
**
*/

/*
** FireFX0 - BlasterFireFX
*/

[FireFX0]

Name			= "BlasterFireFX"
FXName			= "MESH_Sub_Muzzle"  // looks like a ClientFX...ignoring
EjectShells 	= 0
FireSound		= 1
ExitMark		= 0
ExitDebris		= 0
ShellModel		= ""
ShellSkin		= ""
ShellScale		= <2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000>
OldStyleBeamName0	= "LOLBeam"

/************************************************************************
**
**	PROJECTILEFX
**
**	ProjectileFX definitions specify the properties making up a projectile
**	fx record.	This record is used to determine the attributes for a
**	given projectile.
**
**	All ProjectileFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name used in Weapons.txt file.
**
**	FXName (String)
**
**		ClientFX effect to play when the projecile is created.
**
**	SmokeTrail (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if a smoke trail should be created. (1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	SmokeTrailType (Integer)
**
**		Specifies the type of trail to be created if SmokeTrail is set to
**		1.	Valid types are:
**
**			1	Short white smoke trail
**			2	Long white smoke trail
**			3	Short black smoke trail
**
**	Flare (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if a flare should be created. (1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	Light (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if a light should be created. (1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	FlySound (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if a fly sound should be created. (1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	Class (String)
**
**		Specifies the type of projectile class to be created.
**
**	ClassData (String) (OPTIONAL)
**
**		This is the name of an optional record that is used to store
**		extra data that is specific to the projecile class. (See the
**		Disc ProjectileFX defined below, and DiscClassData record
**		for an example).
**
**	Model (String)
**
**		Name of the model associated with the projectile
**
**	ModelScale (Vector)
**
**		The scale of the model.
**
**	Skin (String)
**
**		Name of the skin associated with the projectile
**
**	Sound (String)
**
**		Specifies the sound played while the projectile is active (i.e.,
**		the "flying" sound).
**
**	SoundRadius (Integer)
**
**		The radius of the flying sound (in game units)
**
**	FlareSprite (String)
**
**		Specifies the flare sprite that is attached to the rocket model.
**
**	FlareScale (Float)
**
**		The scale of the flare sprite.
**
**	LightColor (Vector)
**
**		The color of the projectile light.
**
**	LightRadius (Integer)
**
**		The radius of the light (in game units)
**
**	Gravity (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if the projectile is affected by gravity (1 = true,
**		0 = false).
**
**	GravityOverride (Float)
**
**		Specifies the local gravity applied to the projectile (if Gravity above
**		is set to 1).  If GravityOverride is set to 0.0 the global gravity (-2000.0)
**		will be used.  NOTE: specify negative values to have the projectile move
**		down (e.g., -1000.0 is 1/2 the default global gravity).
**
**
**	Elasticity (Float)
**
**		When a projectile that is affected by gravite impacts surfaces,
**		the amount it will bounce back is dependant
**		on the surface type.  This elasticity is an additional modifier for the
**		bounce.  Setting this above 1.0 will make it MORE bouncy, setting it
**		below 1.0 will make it less bouncy.  This value will apply to ALL surfaces
**		it impacts.
**
**	Lifetime (Float)
**
**		How long the projectile is active (i.e., how long it moves until
**		it blows up).
**
**	Velocity (Integer)
**
**		How fast the projectile moves.
**
**	AltVelocity (Integer)
**
**		How fast the projectile moves for Alt-fire.
**
**	EnergyDrainMin (Float)
**	EnergyDrainMax (Float)
**	EnergyDrainSurge (Float)
**
**		How fast the projectile depletes the owner's energy stores (in
**		units/sec).
**
**		The player's weapon efficiency rating has an effect on this
**		drain rate.
**
**	FireOffset (Float)
**
**		Change the start position of the projectile this many units along
**		the direction fired.  This stops projectiles from coming out of
**		the camera.  Example:  a value of 5.0 will change the starting
**		position of the projectile to 5.0 units away from the camera in
**		whatever direction the camera is facing.
**		NOTE: this only affects the player
**
**	CanHitSameKind (Integer)
**
**		Specifies if this projectile can impact other projectiles of the same
**		kind.  (1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	MaxRicochetAngle
**
**		This value will allow for glancing blows against world geometry.
**		If the incident angle of the projectile impact (in relation
**		to the surface, NOT the normal) is equal to or beneath this
**		angle it will ricochet instead.
**
**		(Note: the illustration only works with a nonproportional font)
**			normal
**			   |	 /
**			   |	/ incident direction
**			   |   /
**			   |  /
**			   | /
**			   |/max ricochet angle
**		  -----+-----------------
**
**	RicochetFXName (String)
**
**		The Impact effect (see earlier in this file) to play when the
**		projectile ricochets.
**
**	MaxRicochets (Ingeger)
**
**		The maximum number of times the projectile can ricochet.
**
*/

** - Ball Launcher Projectile

/********************************************************

/************************************************************************
**
** DISCCLASSDATA
**
** DiscClassData definition specifies the properties making up a Disc
** class data recerd.  This record is used to store data specific to
** the CDisc class.
**
** The DiscClassData contains the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		A user friendly name to refrence this DiscClassData record from
**		a ProjectileFx.
**
**	ReturnToOwner (Bool)
**
**		Should the disc return to the owner when done?
**
**	InitialAngle (Float)
**
**		The disc will launch this many degrees to the right (off center
**		from the control line).  These units are in DEGREES.
**		NOTE: these are only used by the player and they are only
**		calculated on the client.
**
**	ReturnVelocity (Float)
**
**		How fast the projectile moves if it returns to its owner.
**
**	ReturnHeightOffset (Float)
**
**		When a returning projectile returns to its owner, it goes toward the
**		owner's position + this Y distance (above the position).  (Only for
**		player).
**
**	ReturnFXName (String)
**
**		Name of a ClientFX to play at the disc when it enters return mode.
**
**	BlockedPVFXName (String)
**
**		Name of a 1st person ClientFX to play when the player successfully
**		blocks.
**
**	DeadlyBlockedPVFXName (String)
**
**		Name of a 1st person ClientFX to play when the player successfully
**		performs a deadly block.
**
**	DestroyedInFlightFXName (String)
**
**		Name of the effect to play on the disc projectile when its owner
**		dies.
**
**	DeflectAttachedFXName (String - name of a client effect)
**
**		The ClientFX to attach to the disc when it is in the Deadly Deflect
**		mode.
**
**	DeadlyDeflectAttachedFXName (String - name of a client effect)
**
**		The ClientFX to attach to the disc when it is in the Deadly Deflect
**		mode.
**
**	DeadlyDeflectSmiteFXName (String - name of a client effect)
**
**		The ClietFX to play when the disc returns to the owner and smites
**		it a deadly blow.
**
**	TurnRate (Float)
**
**		The speed at which the disc can change direction in flight.  Lower
**		values will make the disc's path smoother but make it less responsive
**		to the user.  Higher values will allow the disc to make sharper
**		turns, giving more control but making the disc less smooth.  The
**		units for these values are in DEGREES/SEC.
**
 **	IncidentAngleToControlLine (Float)
 **
 **		The disc tries to steer itself onto an invisible line coming
 **		straight out of the owner.	This will determine the angle the
 **		disc will use to get back to the line.	Higher values will mean
 **		tighter control, lower values will give it a looser feel.  The
 **		units for these values are DEGREES.
 **
 **	IncidentAngleToControlLineDecay (Float)
 **
 **		This is the rate at which the IncidentAngle will decay.  The
 **		IncidentAngle decays while the disc remains in flight so it will
 **		"home in" on the control line.	Higher values will give the
 **		disc a more zig-zaggy eratic feel.	Lower values will give it
 **		a smoother feel, but it will be slower to react to the user's
 **		ministrations.	The units on these values are DEGREES/SECOND.
 **
 **	TargetAngleTrackThreshold (Float- degrees)
 **
 **		** For homing discs only. **  If the disc passes its target
 **		it will enter return mode (after a certain amount of time
 **		has passed, see LostTargetFlightTime).  This angle is the
 **		measure between the velocity of the disc and the direction
 **		of to the target.
 **
 **	LostTargetFlightTime (Float- seconds)
 **
 **		** For homing (enemy) discs only. **  The amount of time before
 **		entering return mode when a homing disc passes its target.
 **		See TargetAngleTrackThreshold to determine when that is.
 **
**	**
**	DISC DEFLECTION
**	**
**
**	DeflectTotalTime (Float: units in seconds)
**
**		Total time that the disc will be deflecting.
**
**	MPDeflectTotalTime (Float: units in seconds)
**
**		Total time that the disc will be deflecting in multiplayer.
**
**	DeflectVelocity (Float: units in distance/sec)
**
**		The velocity of the disc when deflecting.
**
**	**
**	DISC MAGNETIC HOMING
**	**
**
**	Imagine a target (character) exerting a pull on the disc
**	as the disc travels.  Just like a magnet, the pull will
**	get stronger as the disc gets closer to the target.
**
**	MagneticRadius (Float: units in world distance units)
**
**		The radius at which the disc searches for targets to hit.
**
**	MagneticMiddleInfluence (Float: Percentage 0.0 - 1.0)
**
**		How strong the pull is at the center of the area of effect.
**		If this number is maximum (1.0), the disc will try to go
**		straight for the target and ignore all other influences.
**
**	MagneticEdgeInfluence (Float: Percentage 0.0 - 1.0)
**
**		How strong the pull is at the outer edge of the area
**		of effect.  The amount of pull decreases at a
**		constant rate from the middle to the edge value.
**		If this number is maximum (1.0), the disc will try to go
**		straight for the target and ignore all other influences.
**
**	MagneticAngleMax (Float: Degrees)
**
**		The magnetic effect happens only while the target is in
**		"front" of the disc...meaning in the direction of the
**		disc's velocity.  This angle defines half the arc in front
**		of the disc.
**
**	Controlable (Bool)
**
**		Is this disc controlable when released?
**
*/

[DiscClassData0]

Name										= "PrimitiveDiscClassData"
ReturnToOwner								= true
InitialAngle								= 0.0
ReturnVelocity								= 2500.0
ReturnHeightOffset							= 30.0
ReturnFXName								= "disc_return"
BlockedPVFXName								= "disc_PVBlock"
DeadlyBlockedPVFXName						= "DISC_PVBlock_Deadly_Alpha"
DestroyedInFlightFXName						= "DISC_DestroyInFlight"
DeflectAttachedFXName						= ""
DeadlyDeflectAttachedFXName					= "disc_DeflectReturnTail"
DeadlyDeflectSmiteFXName					= "DISC_Deflect_explosion"
TurnRate									= 35.0
IncidentAngleToControlLine					= 20.0
IncidentAngleToControlLineDecay				= 0.0
TargetAngleTrackThreshold					= 90.0
LostTargetFlightTime						= 0.1
DeflectTotalTime							= 2.5
MPDeflectTotalTime							= 2.5
DeflectVelocity								= 500.0
MagneticRadius								= 1000.0
MagneticMiddleInfluence						= 1.0
MagneticEdgeInfluence						= 1.0
MagneticAngleMax							= 60.0
Controlable									= true
MultiplayerLeashLength						= 10000.0

/************************************************************************
**
** CORRUPTICDIMSCLASSDATA
**
** CorrupticDimsClassData definition specifies the properties making up a Disc
** class data recerd.  This record is used to store data specific to
** the CCorrupticDim class.
**
**	Randomness (Float, Percentage 0.0-1.0)
**
**		Percentage chance that it will change position each frame.
**
**	RandomnessRampUpTime (Float, time in seconds)
**
**		The Randomness (above) and the effect of the randomness (the
**		factors below) will increase from 0 to their full value over
**		the amount of time specified here.  If 0 is specified for the
**		time, this field has no effect.
**
**	HorizontalFactor (Float, Distance from line)
**	VerticalFactor (Float, Distance from line)
**
**		The velocity of the Corruptic Dims are constant toward the
**		target, but the projectile itself will bounce around an
**		invisible line from the fire position in the \ection
**		it was shot.  The projectile will look like it is taking
**		a very random path, but it will still be constrained in
**		an imaginary cylinder surrounding the invisible line.
**		Each frame it decides to change position, it will
**		randomly select a new position in the horizontal and vertical
**		plane.  These values specify the maximum distarce from that
**		line.
**		Example:
**				forward velocity = 200 (specified it projectile structure)
**				HorizontalFactor = 30.0
**				VerticalFactor   = 60.0
**			The forward velocity will be 200.  The projectile will bounce
**			randomly 30 units above or below that line, and 60 units to
**			the left or right of the line.  This will remain in effect
**			until it decides to change position again.
**
**	Homing (int: 0 = false; all else = true)
**
**		If this is nonzero, the corruptic dim will "home in" on its target.
**
**	TurnRate (float: units are degrees/sec)
**
**		The maximum number of degrees in a second that the projectile
**		will turn.
**
**
**/

[CorrupticDimsClassData0]
Name							= "BasicCorrupticDimsClassData"
Randomness						= 0.5
RandomnessRampUpTime			= 1.0
HorizontalFactor				= 40.3
VerticalFactor					= 20.3
Homing							= 1
TurnRate						= 30.0

[CorrupticDimsClassData1]

/************************************************************************
**
**	BALLCLASSDATA
**
**	Extra data for TRON's ball (grenade) projectile.
**
**	MinThrowTime (Float: units are seconds)
**
**		This is a threshold.  If the fire button is pressed less than
**		this amount, the default velocity (the velocity specified in
**		the ProjectileFX) is used.  If the fire button is held for
**		more than this time, the velocity will be adjusted depending
**		on how long the button has been pressed for.
**
**	MaxThrowTime (Float: units are seconds)
**
**		This is the maximum amount of time that the fire button can
**		be pressed.  Holding the fire button this long will give
**		the projectile the maximum amount of velocity.
**
**	MinThrowVelocity (Float: units are world units/sec)
**
**		The minimum amount of velocity the ball can have.
**
**	MaxThrowVelocity (Float: units are world units/sec)
**
**		The maximum amount of velocity the ball can have.
**
**	ProximityThreshold (Float: units are in seconds)
**
**		If the ball hits a wall before this time expires, it will
**		stick to the wall and become a proximity bomb instead.
**
**	ProximitySecondsToArm (Float: units are seconds)
**
**		If the ball becomes a proximity bomb, it will be harmless
**		for this many seconds.  After that, it is armed and read
**		to dish out some HURT!
**
**	ProximityDistance (Float: units are in world units)
**
**		If the ball is a proximity bomb, it will detonate if a
**		character comes within this many units.
**
**	PromitityBombEffect (String: name of a ClientFX)
**
**		The ClientFX to play (instead of the normally attached
**		ClientFX) on the object when it is a Proximity Bomb
**		instead of a normal ball.
**
**	RandomAngleAdjust (Float: units are degrees)
**
**		Every update, the velocity will change sideways by a
**		random amount.  This is the maximum angle it will change.
**
**/

[BALLCLASSDATA0]
Name							= "BallClassData"
MinThrowTime					= 0.0
MaxThrowTime					= 0.3
MinThrowVelocity				= 1000.0
MaxThrowVelocity				= 2500.0
ProximityThreshold				= 0.25
ProximitySecondsToArm			= 2.0
ProximityDistance				= 400.0
ProximityBombEffectName			= "BALL_GREN_ProximityFX"
RandomAngleAdjust				= 0.0

/************************************************************************
**
**	PRANKSTERCLASSDATA
**
**	Extra data for TRON's Prankster Bit projectile.
**
**	EliminateTargetsFX (String- FXEd effect)
**
**		FXEd effect to play for the explosion.
**
**	TimeToAcquireTargets (Float- in seconds)
**
**		Amount of time to spend searching for valid targets to zap.
**
**	TimeVictimStasis (Float- in seconds)
**
**		Base amount of time that a victim will stay in "stasis".  This
**		will be offset random offset limited by the TimeVictimStasisRange
**		(see below) like this:  If the base is 5 seconds and the range
**		is 3 seconds, the victim will stay in stasis between 2 and 8
**		seconds.
**
**	TimeVictimStasisRange (Float- in seconds)
**
**		Amount of variation that the victim will stay in stasis.  See
**		TimeVictimStasis above.
**
**	MaxDistance  (Float- in units)
**
**		The max distance to look for victims.
**
**	MaxTargets (Int- amount of victims)
**
**		The maximum number of victims to grab.
**
**	BaseVelocity (Float- in units/second)
**
**		The base value of the velocity the victim will travel to
**		their death.  This value is used in conjunction with
**		VelocityRange (see below) to set a random range at which
**		the velocity will be chosen.  For example:  if the base is
**		500 units/second and the range is 300 units/second, the
**		final velocity will be between 200 units/second and
**		800 units/second.
**
**	VelocityRange (Float- in units/second)
**
**		The amount of variation to the victim's velocity.  See
**		BaseVelocity from above.
**
**	DeathRadius (Float- in units)
**
**		The distance from the Prankster Bit's center that victims
**		will derez.
**
*/

/************************************************************************
**
** SCALEFX
**
** ScaleFX definitions specify the properties making up a model or sprite
** scale fx record.  This record is used to determine the attributes for a
** given model or sprite fx.
**
** All ScaleFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name used in Weapons.txt file.
**
**	Type (Integer)
**
**		Specifies the type of Scale FX to create.  Valid types are:
**
**			0	-	Model
**			1	-	Sprite
**
**	File (String)
**
**		Name of the model or sprite file.
**
**	Skin (String)
**
**		(Models only) Name of the skin.
**
**	InitialScale (Vector)
**
**		The starting model/sprite scale (the model/sprite size is linearly scaled
**		between InitialScale and FinalScale over LifeTime).
**
**	FinalScale (Vector)
**
**		The final model/sprite scale (the model/sprite size is linearly scaled
**		between InitialScale and FinalScale over LifeTime).
**
**	UseColors (Integer)
**
**		If set to 1 the model/sprite will use the colors specified by InitialColor
**		and FinalColor.  If set to 0, the model/sprite will use its normal color.
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	InitialColor (Vector)
**
**		The starting model/sprite color (the model/sprite color is linearly
**		scaled between InitialColor and FinalColor over LifeTime if UseColors = 1).
**
**	FinalColor (Vector)
**
**		The final model/sprite color (the model/sprite color is linearly scaled
**		between InitialColor and FinalColor over LifeTime if UseColors = 1).
**
**	InitialAlpha (Float)
**
**		The starting model alpha (the model alpha is linearly scaled between
**		InitialAlpha and FinalAlpha over LifeTime).
**
**	FinalAlpha (Float)
**
**		The final model/sprite color (the model/sprite alpha is linearly scaled
**		between InitialAlpha and FinalAlpha over LifeTime).
**
**	DirOffset (Float)
**
**		Offset from the impact position where the model/sprite will be created.
**		This value is relative to the direction vector (i.e., along the vector
**		from the impact position to the fire position).  Negative values are
**		closer to the fire position.
**
**	DirROffset (Float)
**
**		Offset from the impact position where the model/sprite will be created.
**		This value is along the right component of the rotation that uses the
**		DirOffset direction as the forward vector (see DirOffset).
**
**	DirUOffset (Float)
**
**		Offset from the impact position where the model/sprite will be created.
**		This value is along the up component of the rotation that uses the
**		DirOffset direction as the forward vector (see DirOffset).
**
**	Velocity (Vector)
**
**		This is a velocity that is applied to the model/sprite over the
**		model/sprite's lifetime.
**
**	LifeTime (Float)
**
**		How long the model/sprite stays around.  Many values are scaled over
**		the lifetime of the model/sprite.
**
**	DelayTime (Float)
**
**		How long after the impact occurs until the model/sprite is created.
**
**	Loop (Integer)
**
**		(Models only) Should the model loop its animation (the first animation
**		is always played) (1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	AlignToSurface (Integer)
**
**		(Sprites only) Should the sprite be aligned with the surface of impact?
**		(1 = true, 0 = false).	NOTE:  This is only used with ImpactFX ScaleFX.
**
**	NoZ (Integer)
**
**		(Sprites only) Should the sprite ignore z reads/writes (i.e., should
**		the sprite draw on top of everything)
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	ReallyClose (Integer)
**
**		(Models only) Should the model draw really close to the camera (like
**		the player-view weapons)?
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	Additive (Integer)
**
**		Should the sprite/model use additive blending?
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	Multiply (Integer)
**
**		Should the sprite/model use multiply blending?
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	Chromakey (Integer)
**
**		Is the model chromakeyed (Models only)
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	Rotate (Integer)
**
**		Should the sprite/model rotate around the forward vector (NOTE: if
**		you set this on a sprite be default it will align with the forward
**		vector.  If you want it to face the camera, you must set the FaceCamera
**		property to 1).
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	FaceCamera (Integer)
**
**		Should a rotating sprite (see Rotate above) face (forward vector) the
**		camera.  (NOTE: this is only used with rotating sprite scale fx).
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	RotationAxis (Integer)
**
**		Which axis should a model rotate around . (NOTE: this is only used with
**		rotating model scale fx).
**		(0 = forward axis, 1 = up axis, 2 = right/left axis)
**
**	MinRotVel (Float)
**
**		The minimum rotation velocity.	This is only used if Rotate (see above)
**		is set to 1.  The rotation velocity used by the scale fx is a random
**		value between MinRotVel and MaxRotVel.
**
**		NOTE: A negative rotation velocity will cause the scale fx to rotate
**		to the left and a positive rotation velocity will cause the scale fx
**		to rotate to the right.  If you want to randomly rotate the fx left
**		or right you can do this by setting MinRotVel = -MaxRotVel (e.g.,
**		MinRotVel = -2.0 and MaxRotVel = 2.0)
**
**	MaxRotVel (Float)
**
**		The maximum rotation velocity.	This is only used if Rotate (see above)
**		is set to 1.  The rotation velocity used by the scale fx is a random
**		value between MinRotVel and MaxRotVel.
**
**		NOTE: A negative rotation velocity will cause the scale fx to rotate
**		to the left and a positive rotation velocity will cause the scale fx
**		to rotate to the right.  If you want to randomly rotate the fx left
**		or right you can do this by setting MinRotVel = -MaxRotVel (e.g.,
**		MinRotVel = -2.0 and MaxRotVel = 2.0)
**
**	MenuLayer (Integer?)
**
**		Apparently from TO2.  Presumably on orderering on scale sprites
**		in the menus to determine what is drawn on top of what (no docs
**		in TO2).  Not sure what low or high values signify.
**
*/

/*
** ScaleFX0 -  Interface Main Menu background sprite 1
*/

[ScaleFX0]

Name			= "InterfaceSpr1"
Type			= 1
File			= "interface\menu\Spr\mainmenu2.spr"
Skin			= ""
InitialScale	= <0.6, 0.6, 0.6>
FinalScale		= <0.6, 0.6, 0.6>
UseColors		= 1

/************************************************************************
**
** PSHOWERFX
**
** PShowerFX definitions specify the properties making up a particle shower
** fx record.  This record is used to determine the attributes for a
** particle shower special fx.
**
** All PShowerFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name.
**
**	Texture (String)
**
**		Name of the texture (or sprite) used by the particle system.
**
**	MinParticles (Integer)
**
**		Minimum number of particles to create (a random number between
**		MinParticles and MaxParticles will be created).
**
**	MaxParticles (Integer)
**
**		Maximum number of particles to create (a random number between
**		MinParticles and MaxParticles will be created).
**
**	Color1 (Vector)
**
**		The beginning range of the particle colors (a random value between
**		Color1 and Color2 is used)
**
**	Color2 (Vector)
**
**		The ending range of the particle colors (a random value between
**		Color1 and Color2 is used)
**
**	MinVel (Float)
**
**		The minimum velocity of the particles (a random value between MinVel
**		and MaxVel is assigned to each particle).
**
**	MaxVel (Float)
**
**		The maximum velocity of the particles (a random value between MinVel
**		and MaxVel is assigned to each particle).
**
**	DirOffset (Float)
**
**		Offset from the impact position where the fx will be created.
**		This value is relative to the direction vector (i.e., along the vector
**		from the impact position to the fire position).  Negative values are
**		closer to the fire position.
**
**	MinDuration (Float)
**
**		Minimum duration the particle system lasts (a random value between
**		MinDuration and MaxDuration is used).  Alpha is faded from 1 to 0
**		over the duration.
**
**	MaxDuration (Float)
**
**		Maximum duration the particle system lasts (a random value between
**		MinDuration and MaxDuration is used).  Alpha is faded from 1 to 0
**		over the duration.
**
**	EmissionRadius (Float)
**
**		The radius (around the direction the shower is moving) that particles
**		will be added to the system.
**
**	Radius (Float)
**
**		The radius of each particle in the system.
**
**	Gravity (Float)
**
**		The gravity of the particle system (Note: negative is down.  Normal
**		world gravity is -500).
**
**	Additive (Integer)
**
**		Should the particle system use additive blending?
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	Multiply (Integer)
**
**		Should the particle system use multiply blending?
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
*/

/*
** PShowerFX0 - Blood particle shower (Flesh impacts)
*/

Name			= "Blood"
Texture 		= "SFX\Particle\Blood_4.dtx"
MinParticles	= 1

/************************************************************************
**
** POLYDEBRISFX
**
** PolyDebrisFX definitions specify the properties making up a poly
** debris fx record.  This record is used to determine the attributes
** for a poly debris special fx.
**
** All PolyDebrisFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name.
**
**	Texture (String)
**
**		Name of the texture used on the canvas.
**
**	Style (Integer)
**
**		The style of debris to create.	Valid types are:
**
**			0	- Triangle1 	(Big to small)
**			1	- Triangle2 	(Small to big)
**			2	- Diamond		(Small to Small)
**			3	- Rectangular	(Constant)
**			4	- Random		(All of the above)
**
**	MinDebris (Integer)
**
**		Minimum number of debris polies to create (a random number between
**		MinDebris and MaxDebris will be created).
**
**	MaxDebris (Integer)
**
**		Maximum number of debris polies to create (a random number between
**		MinDebris and MaxDebris will be created).
**
**	MinColor1 (Vector)
**
**		The starting debris polies color is a random value between
**		MinColor1 and MaxColor1.
**
**	MaxColor1 (Vector)
**
**		The starting debris polies color is a random value between
**		MinColor1 and MaxColor1.
**
**	MinColor2 (Vector)
**
**		The ending debris polies color is a random value between
**		MinColor2 and MaxColor2.
**
**	MaxColor2 (Vector)
**
**		The ending debris polies color is a random value between
**		MinColor2 and MaxColor2.
**
**	Additive (Integer)
**
**		Should additive blending be used on the polies (1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	Multiply (Integer)
**
**		Should multiply blending be used on the polies (1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	ShowTrail (Integer)
**
**		Should a trail be left behind the debris (1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	MinVel (Vector)
**
**		The minimum velocity of the debris (a random value between MinVel
**		and MaxVel is assigned to each debris).  The velocity is directional
**		with the Y component mapping to the forward direction of movement.
**
**	MaxVel (Vector)
**
**		The maximum velocity of the debris (a random value between MinVel
**		and MaxVel is assigned to each debris).  The velocity is directional
**		with the Y component mapping to the forward direction of movement.
**
**	DirOffset (Float)
**
**		Offset from the impact position where the fx will be created.
**		This value is relative to the direction vector (i.e., along the vector
**		from the impact position to the fire position).  Negative values are
**		closer to the fire position.
**
**	MinDebrisOffset (Vector)
**
**		The minimum offset (from the origin of the debris) where each poly
**		debris item is created.  A random value between MinDebrisOffset
**		and MinDebrisOffset is assigned to each debris.  NOTE:	The offsets
**		are in world coordinates, so the x and z components of the vector
**		should always be the same (unless you want the fx to always align
**		to a world axis).
**
**	MaxDebrisOffset (Vector)
**
**		The minimum offset (from the origin of the debris) where each poly
**		debris item is created.  A random value between MinDebrisOffset
**		and MinDebrisOffset is assigned to each debris.  NOTE:	The offsets
**		are in world coordinates, so the x and z components of the vector
**		should always be the same (unless you want the fx to always align
**		to a world axis).
**
**	DirOffsetOnly (Integer)
**
**		Should the debris be offset only along the direction it will travel
**		(1 = true, 0 = false).	If this is set to 1, only the Y component of
**		MinDebrisOffset/MaxDebrisOffset will be used to deterine the radius
**		away from the origin of the fx where the poly debris will be created.
**
**	MinDuration (Float)
**
**		Minimum duration the debris lasts (a random value between
**		MinDuration and MaxDuration is used).  Alpha is faded from InitialAlpha
**		to FinalAlpha over the duration.
**
**	MaxDuration (Float)
**
**		Maximum duration the debris lasts (a random value between
**		MinDuration and MaxDuration is used).  Alpha is faded from InitialAlpha
**		to FinalAlpha over the duration.
**
**	InitialAlpha (Float)
**
**		The starting debris alpha (the debris alpha is linearly scaled between
**		InitialAlpha and FinalAlpha over the duration).
**
**	FinalAlpha (Float)
**
**		The final debris alpha (the debris alpha is linearly scaled between
**		InitialAlpha and FinalAlpha over the duration).
**
**	MinWidth (Float)
**
**		The minimum "width" of the poly debris (a random width between MinWidth
**		and MaxWidth is used).
**
**	MaxWidth (Float)
**
**		The maximum "width" of the poly debris (a random width between MinWidth
**		and MaxWidth is used).
**
**	MinLength (Float)
**
**		The minimum "length" of the poly debris (a random width between MinLength
**		and MaxLength is used).
**
**	MaxLength (Float)
**
**		The maximum "length" of the poly debris (a random width between MinLength
**		and MaxLength is used).
**
**	MinBounce (Integer)
**
**		The minimum number of bounces the debris will do before it stops moving
**		(a random value between MinBounce and MaxBounce is used).
**
**	MaxBounce(Integer)
**
**		The maximum number of bounces the debris will do before it stops moving
**		(a random value between MinBounce and MaxBounce is used).
**
**	GravityScale (Float)
**
**		How much the gravity on the debris should be scaled by (multiplier -
**		i.e., 0.5 is 1/2 normal gravity, 2.0 is twice normal gravity).
**
**	MinWorldVel (Vector)
**	MaxWorldVel (Vector)
**
**		Support for a minimum and maximum world space velocity for debris and
**		polydebris. In the attributes file it is simply MinWorldVel and
**		MaxWorldVel.  It will then pick a random value between that to add
**		to the velocity of the debris. This way you can make debris pop upwards.
**
*/

/*
** PolyDebrisFX0 - Sparks poly debris
*/

[PolyDebrisFX0]

Name			= "Sparks"
Texture 		= "sfx\test\fxtest40.dtx"
Style			= 3
MinDebris		= 8
MaxDebris		= 16
MinColor1		= <255.000000, 255.000000, 255.000000>
MaxColor1		= <255.000000, 255.000000, 255.000000>
MinColor2		= <255.000000, 255.000000, 255.000000>
MaxColor2		= <255.000000, 255.000000, 255.000000>
MinVel			= <-300.000000, 150.000000, -300.000000>
MaxVel			= <300.000000, 300.000000, 300.000000>
Additive		= 1
Multiply		= 0
ShowTrail		= 1
DirOffset		= 0.0
MinDebrisOffset = <0.0, 0.0, 0.0>
MaxDebrisOffset = <0.0, 0.0, 0.0>
DirOffsetOnly	= 0
GravityScale	= 1.0
MinDuration 	= 0.10000
MaxDuration 	= 0.50000
InitialAlpha	= 0.900000
FinalAlpha		= 0.000000
MinWidth		= 0.750000
MaxWidth		= 3.000000
MinLength		= 1.000000
MaxLength		= 1.000000
MinBounce		= 1
MaxBounce		= 3
MinWorldVel		= <0.0, 0.0, 0.0>
MaxWorldVel		= <0.0, 0.0, 0.0>

/*
** PolyDebrisFX2 - Stone poly debris
*/

/************************************************************************
**
** PEXPLFX
**
** PExplFX definitions specify the properties making up a particle
** explosion fx record.  This record is used to determine the attributes
** for a particle explosion fx.
**
** All PExplFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name used in Weapons.txt file.
**
**	File (String)
**
**		Name of the particle texture (or sprite).
**
**	PosOffset (Vector)
**
**		Offset from the impact position for the particle explosion to be
**		created.
**
**	NumPerPuff (Integer)
**
**		Number of particles added for each "puff"
**
**	NumEmmitters (Integer)
**
**		Number of particles emmitters in the explosion.
**
**	NumSteps (Integer)
**
**		Number of particle puffs per time step.
**
**	CreateDebris (Integer)
**
**		If set to 1 if debris should be created.
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	RotateDebris (Integer)
**
**		If set to 1 if the debris should be rotated.
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	IgnoreWind (Integer)
**
**		Should the particles ignore the world wind velocity.
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	DoBubbles (Integer)
**
**		Should the particles turn into bubbles when in liquids (i.e. underwater)
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	Color1 (Vector)
**
**		The particles will have colors between Color1 and Color2.
**
**	Color2 (Vector)
**
**		The particles will have colors between Color1 and Color2.
**
**	MinVel (Vector)
**
**		The minimum velocity of the particle emmitters (the Y velocity is mapped
**		to the impact surface normal).
**
**	MaxVel (Vector)
**
**		The maximum velocity of the particle emmiters (the Y velocity is mapped
**		to the impact surface normal).
**
**	MinDriftVel (Vector)
**
**		The minimum drift velocity of the particle explosion (a random velocity
**		between MinDriftVel and MaxDriftVel will be applied to each "puff").
**
**	MaxDriftVel (Vector)
**
**		The maximum drift velocity of the particle explosion (a random velocity
**		between MinDriftVel and MaxDriftVel will be applied to each "puff").
**
**	LifeTime (Float)
**
**		How long the particles stay around.
**
**	FadeTime (Float)
**
**		How long after the particle explosion is created before the particles
**		are linearly faded away (must be less than LifeTime).
**
**	OffsetTime (Float)
**
**		How offten a new particle "puff" is created.
**
**	Radius (Float)
**
**		The particle radius.
**
**	Gravity (Float)
**
**		Gravity applied to all the particles in the system.
**
**	Additive (Integer)
**
**		Should the particle system use additive blending?
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	Multiply (Integer)
**
**		Should the particle system use multiply blending?
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
*/

/*
** PExplFX0 - Rocket Particle Explosion
*/

[PExplFX0]

Name			= "RocketPExpl1"
File			= "SFX\Particle\Fire2.dtx" // "SFX\Particle\Fire4.dtx"
PosOffset		= <0.000000, 0.000000, 0.000000>
NumPerPuff		= 6
NumEmitters 	= 10
NumSteps		= 2

MaxVel			= <500.000000, 500.000000, 500.000000>

MaxDriftVel 	= <0.000000, 6.000000, 0.000000>

/************************************************************************
**
** DLIGHTFX
**
** DLightFX definitions specify the properties making up a dynamic light
** fx record.  This record is used to determine the attributes
** for a dynamic light fx.
**
** All DLightFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name used in Weapons.txt file.
**
**	Color (Vector)
**
**		The color of the dynamic light
**
**	MinRadius (Float)
**
**		The minimum radius of the light (the light will be created with this
**		radius)
**
**	MaxRadius (Float)
**
**		The maximum radius of the light.
**
**	MinTime (Float)
**
**		The time the light will remain at the minimum radius.
**
**	MaxTime (Float)
**
**		The time the light will remain at the maximum radius.
**
**	RampUpTime (Float)
**
**		The time it takes for the light to ramp from MinRadius to MaxRadius.
**
**	RampDownTime (Float)
**
**		The time it takes for the light to ramp from MaxRadius to 0.
**
*/

/*
** DLightFX0 - Rocket explosion light
*/

Name			= "Rocket"
Color			= <150.000000, 140.000000, 130.000000>
MinRadius		= 50
MaxRadius		= 125

RampDownTime	= 0.300000



/************************************************************************
**
** PVFX
**
** PVFX definitions specify the properties making up a player-view fx.
**
** All PVFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name used in Weapons.txt file.
**
**	Socket (String)
**
**		Specifies the name of the player-view model socket to attach the
**		fx to.
**
**	ScaleName# (String)  (OPTIONAL) [10 MAX]
**
**		Specifies the optional name of scale fx to create for this fx.
**		The value of this property MUST correspond to the name of a ScaleFX
**		defined in this file.  If the fx uses multiple scale fx types, you
**		may specify multiple ScaleName properties.	For example:
**
**			ScaleName0	= "LighterSprite1"
**			ScaleName1	= "LighterSprite2"
**			...
**			ScaleName9	= "LighterSprite9"
**
**	DLightName# (String)  (OPTIONAL) [10 MAX]
**
**		Specifies the optional name of dynamic light fx to create for this
**		fx.  The value of this property MUST correspond to the name
**		of a DLightFX defined in this file.  If the fx uses multiple dynamic
**		light fx types, you may specify multiple DLightName properties.
**		For example:
**
**			DLightName0 = "LighterLight1"
**			DLightName1 = "LighterLight2"
**			...
**			DLightName9 = "LighterLight9"
**
**	SoundName# (String)  (OPTIONAL) [10 MAX]
**
**		Specifies the optional name of a sound fx to create for this
**		fx.  The value of this property MUST correspond to the name
**		of a SoundFX defined in this file.	If the fx uses multiple
**		sound fx types, you may specify multiple SoundName properties.
**		For example:
**
**			SoundName0 = "LighterSound1"
**			SoundName1 = "LighterSound2"
**			...
**			SoundName9 = "LighterSound9"
**
*/


/*
** PVFX0 - Test FX
*/

Name				= "DiscTest"


/************************************************************************
**
** ParticleMuzzleFX
**
** ParticleMuzzleFX definitions specify the properties making up a particle
** muzzle flash fx.
**
** All ParticleMuzzleFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name used in Weapons.txt file.
**
**	File (String)
**
**		Name of the particle sprite/dtx used by the particle system.
**
**	MaxScale (Float)
**
**		The max scale (in y) for the particle system.
**
**	Radius (Float)
**
**		The size of each particle.
**
**	Length (Float)
**
**		The length of the system (away from the weapon)
**
**	Duration (Float)
**
**		Length of time the system should stay around.
**
**	NumParticles (Integer)
**
**		Number of particles in the system
**
**	Color1 (Vector)
**
**		The beginning range of the particle colors (a random value between
**		Color1 and Color2 is used)
**
**	Color2 (Vector)
**
**		The ending range of the particle colors (a random value between
**		Color1 and Color2 is used)
**
**	Additive (Integer)
**
**		Should the particle system use additive blending?
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
**	Multiply (Integer)
**
**		Should the particle system use multiply blending?
**		(1 = true, 0 = false)
**
*/

** ParticleMuzzleFX0 - PV_P38

**

**		to the name of a ScaleFX record defined above.

**

**

**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name used in Weapons.txt file.
**
**	Texture (String)
**
**		Name of the texture used on the canvas.
**
**	Duration (Float)
**
**		How long the beam lasts.
**
**	Width (Float)
**
**		The beam's width (in game units).
**
**	InitialAlpha (Float)
**
**		The beam's starting alpha
**
**	FinalAlpha (Float)
**
**		The beams's ending alpha.
**
**	Color (Vector)
**
**		The beams's color.
**
**	AlignFlat (Integer)
**
**		Should the beam be aligned flat (horizontal in the world) (1=true, 0=false)
**
**	AlignUp (Integer)
**
**		Should the beam be aligned up (vertical in the world) (1=true, 0=false)
**
*/

//Texture			= "sfx\beams\skins\laser.dtx"

/************************************************************************
**
** SoundFX
**
** SoundFX definitions specify the properties making up a sound fx
**
** All SoundFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name used to identify this fx.
**
**	File (String)
**
**		Name of the sound file.
**
**	Loop (Integer)
**
**		Should the sound loop (1=true, 0=false)
**
**	Radius (Float)
**
**		Specifies the radius of the sound (ignored for player-view sounds)
**
**	PitchShift (Float)
**
**		Specifies the radius of the sound.
**
*/

/************************************************************************
**
** PusherFX
**
** PusherFX definitions specify the properties making up a pusher fx
**
** All PusherFX definitins should contain the following properties:
**
**	Name (String)
**
**		User friendly name used to identify this fx.
**
**	Radius (Float)
**
**		The radius of effect
**
**	StartDelay (Float)
**
**		Delay before the effect starts
**
**	Duration (Float)
**
**		How long the effect lasts
**
**	Strength (Float)
**
**		Velocity added each frame based on the distance to center of the pushed
**		object
**
*/

/************************************************************************
**
** SPRINKLEFX
**
** Name (String)
**
**	Userfriendly name for the SprinkleFX
**
** FileName (String)
**
**	The file to be used as the sprinkles can be model (.ltb), texture (.dtx)
**	or sprite (.spr)
**
** SkinName (String)
**
**	If FileName is a model then SkinName is the skin for that model
**
** Count (Integer)
**
**	How many sprinkles are shown.
**
** Speed (Float)
**
**	How fast are the sprinkles moving
**
** Size (Float)
**
**
** SpawnRadius (Float)
**
**	How far around the player will the Sprinkles spawn
**
** ColorMin (Vector)
**
**	Minimum color value of the Sprinkles
**
** ColorMax (Vector)
**
**	Maximum color value of the Sprinkles
**
** AnglesVel (Vector)
**
*/
